27/02/2026, 02:43 - Dimp: 😊 Sounds like you're having charger issues!

## Warranty Claim:
Since the replacement charger stopped working within 2 months (again within the 1-year warranty period), you can likely claim warranty again.

## Why:
- The replacement was likely under the original 1-year warranty.
- If the product failed again within the warranty period, you're entitled to another repair/replacement.

Check the warranty terms for specifics like "replacement warranty" rules. Best to contact the seller/manufacturer ASAP 😊
